### [36] [SAND-Math: Using LLMs to Generate Novel, Difficult and Useful Mathematics Questions and Answers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.20527)
*Chaitanya Manem,Pratik Prabhanjan Brahma,Prakamya Mishra,Zicheng Liu,Emad Barsoum*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLM在数学推理方面需求日益增长，但缺乏复杂数学问题的训练数据。本文提出了SAND-Math合成数据生成管线，通过“难度提升”步骤生成高质量、高难度数学问题。实验证明，使用少量SAND-Math数据可显著提升模型性能，AIME25基准提升17.85分，并且“难度提升”步骤能有效提高问题难度和模型表现。该管线为构建高效数学推理LLM提供了实用工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在数学推理方面的能力需求不断增长，但现有的模型常受限于高质量、复杂数学问题的训练数据稀缺，这阻碍了高性能数学LLM的发展。

Method: 提出SAND-Math（合成、增强、新颖、困难数学问题及解决方案）管线。该管线首先从头开始合成高质量问题，然后通过新提出的“难度提升”步骤系统性地增加问题难度。

Result: 1. 在AIME25基准测试中，使用500个样本的SAND-Math数据集对强基线模型进行增强，性能显著提升，比次优合成数据集高出17.85个绝对百分点。 2. 专门的消融研究表明，“难度提升”过程将平均问题难度从5.02提升到5.98，并将AIME25结果从46.38%提升到49.23%。

Conclusion: SAND-Math管线，包括完整生成流程、最终数据集以及微调模型，为构建高效、强大的数学推理LLM提供了一个实用且可扩展的工具集，有效解决了高质量数学训练数据稀缺的问题。

Abstract: The demand for Large Language Models (LLMs) at multiple scales, capable of
sophisticated and sound mathematical reasoning, continues to grow. However, the
development of performant mathematical LLMs is often bottlenecked by the
scarcity of useful training data containing problems with significant
complexity. We introduce \textbf{SAND-Math} (\textbf{S}ynthetic
\textbf{A}ugmented \textbf{N}ovel and \textbf{D}ifficult Mathematics problems
and solutions), a pipeline that addresses this by first synthesizing
high-quality problems from scratch and then systematically elevating their
complexity via a our newly proposed \textbf{Difficulty Hiking} step. We
demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach through two key findings:
\textbf{(1)} Augmenting a strong post-training baseline with a small 500-sample
SAND-Math dataset significantly boosts performance, outperforming the next-best
synthetic dataset by $\uparrow$ 17.85 absolute points on AIME25 benchmark.
\textbf{(2)} In a dedicated ablation study, we show the effectiveness of our
Difficulty Hiking process in increasing average problem difficulty from 5.02 to
5.98. This step consequently lifts AIME25 results from 46.38\% to 49.23\%. The
full generation pipeline, final dataset, and a fine-tuned model form a
practical and scalable toolkit for building capable and efficient mathematical
reasoning LLMs.

</details>


### [37] [LAWCAT: Efficient Distillation from Quadratic to Linear Attention with Convolution across Tokens for Long Context Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.18467)
*Zeyu Liu,Souvik Kundu,Lianghao Jiang,Anni Li,Srikanth Ronanki,Sravan Bodapati,Gourav Datta,Peter A. Beerel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Transformer 模型的二次计算复杂度是处理长序列的瓶颈。LAWCAT 提出了一种名为 LAWCAT（Linear Attention with Convolution Across Time）的新型线性化框架，通过整合因果 Conv1D 层和归一化门控线性注意力，能够有效地将预训练 Transformer 的能力迁移到线性注意力架构中，从而实现高效的长上下文处理。实验表明，LAWCAT 能够显著扩展模型的有效上下文窗口，同时在推理速度上优于 FlashAttention-2，且所需的预训练数据量极少，为边缘部署提供了高效的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Transformer 模型虽然在多个领域表现优异，但其计算复杂度随序列长度呈二次方增长，这在对延迟敏感的长上下文应用中成为主要瓶颈。尽管已有线性复杂度的替代方案，但从头开始训练它们仍需要大量计算资源。因此，需要一种能够有效迁移预训练 Transformer 能力到线性注意力架构的框架，以克服这些限制。

Method: LAWCAT 框架整合了两种关键技术：1. 因果 Conv1D 层：用于增强局部依赖性建模。2. 归一化门控线性注意力：用于提高在不同上下文长度下的泛化能力。该框架旨在高效地将预训练 Transformer 的能力迁移到一个性能优越的线性注意力架构中。实验在 Mistral-7B 和 Llama3.2-1B 等模型上进行，评估了其在长上下文任务（如 passkey retrieval、S-NIAH 和 BABIlong）上的表现，并与 FlashAttention-2 进行了速度比较。

Result: 实验结果显示，通过在仅 1K 序列长度上对 Mistral-7B 进行蒸馏，LAWCAT 模型在长达 22K 的 token 上仍能保持超过 90% 的 passkey retrieval 准确率，显著扩展了其有效上下文窗口。Llama3.2-1B 的 LAWCAT 变体在 S-NIAH 1&2&3 任务（1K-8K 上下文长度）和 BABIlong 基准测试（QA2&QA3，0K-16K 上下文长度）上取得了具有竞争力的性能，并且与预训练模型相比，所需的预训练 token 数量不到 0.1%。此外，LAWCAT 在超过 8K 序列长度时的预填充速度优于 FlashAttention-2。

Conclusion: LAWCAT 提供了一种高效的方法，能够将强大的 Transformer 能力迁移到线性注意力模型中，实现高性能和长上下文处理能力，特别适合边缘部署。它显著减少了对大量长序列训练数据和计算资源的需求。研究结果表明，LAWCAT 能够有效扩展模型的上下文长度，并在推理速度上具有优势。未来的工作可以进一步探索 LAWCAT 在更多下游任务上的应用，并优化其架构以适应更广泛的硬件平台。

Abstract: Although transformer architectures have achieved state-of-the-art performance
across diverse domains, their quadratic computational complexity with respect
to sequence length remains a significant bottleneck, particularly for
latency-sensitive long-context applications. While recent linear-complexity
alternatives are increasingly powerful, effectively training them from scratch
is still resource-intensive. To overcome these limitations, we propose LAWCAT
(Linear Attention with Convolution Across Time), a novel linearization
framework designed to efficiently transfer the capabilities of pre-trained
transformers into a performant linear attention architecture. LAWCAT integrates
causal Conv1D layers to enhance local dependency modeling and employs
normalized gated linear attention to improve generalization across varying
context lengths. Our comprehensive evaluations demonstrate that, distilling
Mistral-7B with only 1K-length sequences yields over 90\% passkey retrieval
accuracy up to 22K tokens, significantly extending its effective context
window. Similarly, Llama3.2-1B LAWCAT variant achieves competitive performance
on S-NIAH 1\&2\&3 tasks (1K-8K context length) and BABILong benchmark
(QA2\&QA3, 0K-16K context length), requiring less than 0.1\% pre-training
tokens compared with pre-training models. Furthermore, LAWCAT exhibits faster
prefill speeds than FlashAttention-2 for sequences exceeding 8K tokens. LAWCAT
thus provides an efficient pathway to high-performance, long-context linear
models suitable for edge deployment, reducing reliance on extensive
long-sequence training data and computational resources. Code is released at:
https://github.com/zeyuliu1037/LAWCAT

</details>


### [38] [Constraint Satisfaction Approaches to Wordle: Novel Heuristics and Cross-Lexicon Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.02855)
*Jahidul Arafat,Fariha Tasmin,Sanjaya Poudel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究首次将Wordle游戏视为一个约束满足问题（CSP），并提出了两种新颖的约束感知求解策略：CSP感知熵和概率CSP。与现有方法相比，这两种策略在猜测次数、运行时间和噪声鲁棒性方面均有显著提升，并在跨语言验证中表现出良好的泛化能力。研究结果表明，原则性的CSP技术在结构化谜题求解领域优于传统的基于信息论和学习的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Wordle求解器主要依赖信息论熵最大化或基于频率的启发式方法，缺乏对约束条件的正式处理。这导致在处理Wordle这类具有丰富算法特性的约束满足问题时，效果不够理想。本研究旨在弥补这一不足，提出一种更系统、更有效的CSP方法来解决Wordle问题，并探索其在其他类似结构化谜题求解领域的潜力。

Method: 本研究提出了两种新颖的CSP方法来解决Wordle问题：1. CSP感知熵：该方法在约束传播后计算信息增益，而不是在原始候选词集上进行计算，从而更准确地评估每个猜测的有效性。2. 概率CSP框架：该框架结合了贝叶斯词频先验和逻辑约束，通过集成概率模型和逻辑推理来优化词语选择。研究评估了这两种方法在2315个英语单词词汇上的表现，并进行了10%噪声下的鲁棒性分析。此外，还在500个西班牙语单词的词汇上进行了跨语言验证，以评估方法的泛化能力。实验设置包括与Forward Checking等基线方法的性能对比，以及运行时间和成功率等指标的测量。

Result: 在2315个英语单词的词汇上，CSP感知熵算法平均只需要3.54次猜测即可成功，成功率为99.9%，相比Forward Checking算法，猜测次数显著减少了1.7%（t=-4.82, p<0.001, Cohen's d=0.07），且运行速度提高了46%（平均每次猜测耗时12.9毫秒，而Forward Checking为23.7毫秒）。在存在10%噪声的情况下，CSP感知熵方法仍保持了5.3个百分点的优势（29.0% vs 23.7%, p=0.041）。概率CSP框架在0-20%的噪声水平下均实现了100%的成功率，这得益于其内置的约束恢复机制。在500个西班牙语单词的词汇上进行跨语言验证时，该方法在没有进行任何特定语言调整的情况下，成功率达到了88%，尽管与英语词汇相比存在11.2个百分点的差距（p<0.001, Fisher's exact test），这表明核心CSP原理可以跨语言应用。研究还提供了具有91%代码覆盖率的开源实现，包含34个单元测试，为CSP研究提供了可复现的基础设施。

Conclusion: 本研究通过将Wordle游戏形式化为CSP问题，并提出CSP感知熵和概率CSP等新颖的约束感知求解策略，显著提升了Wordle的求解效率和鲁棒性。实验结果表明，这些基于原则性的CSP技术在平均猜测次数、运行时间和噪声处理方面均优于传统的基于信息论和学习的方法。此外，跨语言验证也证明了该方法具有良好的泛化能力。该研究不仅为结构化谜题求解领域设定了新的性能基准，而且其开源实现为未来的CSP研究提供了宝贵的基础设施。未来的工作可以进一步探索该方法在更复杂的CSP问题和不同类型的谜题中的应用。

Abstract: Wordle presents an algorithmically rich testbed for constraint satisfaction
problem (CSP) solving. While existing solvers rely on information-theoretic
entropy maximization or frequency-based heuristics without formal constraint
treatment, we present the first comprehensive CSP formulation of Wordle with
novel constraint-aware solving strategies. We introduce CSP-Aware Entropy,
computing information gain after constraint propagation rather than on raw
candidate sets, and a Probabilistic CSP framework integrating Bayesian
word-frequency priors with logical constraints. Through evaluation on 2,315
English words, CSP-Aware Entropy achieves 3.54 average guesses with 99.9%
success rate, a statistically significant 1.7% improvement over Forward
Checking (t=-4.82, p<0.001, Cohen's d=0.07) with 46% faster runtime (12.9ms
versus 23.7ms per guess). Under 10% noise, CSP-aware approaches maintain 5.3
percentage point advantages (29.0% versus 23.7%, p=0.041), while Probabilistic
CSP achieves 100% success across all noise levels (0-20%) through constraint
recovery mechanisms. Cross-lexicon validation on 500 Spanish words demonstrates
88% success with zero language-specific tuning, validating that core CSP
principles transfer across languages despite an 11.2 percentage point gap from
linguistic differences (p<0.001, Fisher's exact test). Our open-source
implementation with 34 unit tests achieving 91% code coverage provides
reproducible infrastructure for CSP research. The combination of formal CSP
treatment, constraint-aware heuristics, probabilistic-logical integration,
robustness analysis, and cross-lexicon validation establishes new performance
benchmarks demonstrating that principled constraint satisfaction techniques
outperform classical information-theoretic and learning-based approaches for
structured puzzle-solving domains.

</details>


### [39] [AWARE, Beyond Sentence Boundaries: A Contextual Transformer Framework for Identifying Cultural Capital in STEM Narratives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.04983)
*Khalid Mehtab Khan,Anagha Kulkarni*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了AWARE框架，通过增强Transformer模型对学生反思文本中文化资本（CC）主题的领域、上下文和类别重叠的感知能力，显著提高了主题识别的准确性，特别是在处理嵌入在叙事中而非直接出现的细微主题方面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别学生反思中的文化资本（CC）主题对于促进课堂公平至关重要。然而，像志向或家庭支持等主题常融入叙事之中，而非作为直接关键词出现，这给孤立处理句子的标准自然语言处理（NLP）模型带来了检测挑战。根本原因在于标准模型在通用语料库上进行预训练，缺乏对数据特有的领域语言和叙事语境的认知。

Method: 研究引入了AWARE框架，一个包含三个核心组成部分来系统性地增强Transformer模型在此任务上的感知能力：1）领域感知，调整模型词汇以适应学生反思的语言风格；2）上下文感知，生成能够感知整个论文语境的句子嵌入；3）类别重叠感知，采用多标签策略识别单个句子中主题的共存现象。

Result: 实验结果表明，通过明确增强模型对输入特性的感知能力，AWARE框架在Macro-F1指标上比强大的基线模型提高了2.1个百分点，并在所有主题上显示出显著的改进。

Conclusion: AWARE提供了一种稳健且可推广的方法，适用于任何意义依赖于叙事语境的文本分类任务。该研究强调了在特定领域任务中增强模型对领域语言、上下文依赖性和多标签特性的理解的重要性。

Abstract: Identifying cultural capital (CC) themes in student reflections can offer
valuable insights that help foster equitable learning environments in
classrooms. However, themes such as aspirational goals or family support are
often woven into narratives, rather than appearing as direct keywords. This
makes them difficult to detect for standard NLP models that process sentences
in isolation. The core challenge stems from a lack of awareness, as standard
models are pre-trained on general corpora, leaving them blind to the
domain-specific language and narrative context inherent to the data. To address
this, we introduce AWARE, a framework that systematically attempts to improve a
transformer model's awareness for this nuanced task. AWARE has three core
components: 1) Domain Awareness, adapting the model's vocabulary to the
linguistic style of student reflections; 2) Context Awareness, generating
sentence embeddings that are aware of the full essay context; and 3) Class
Overlap Awareness, employing a multi-label strategy to recognize the
coexistence of themes in a single sentence. Our results show that by making the
model explicitly aware of the properties of the input, AWARE outperforms a
strong baseline by 2.1 percentage points in Macro-F1 and shows considerable
improvements across all themes. This work provides a robust and generalizable
methodology for any text classification task in which meaning depends on the
context of the narrative.

### [40] [Revisiting Long-context Modeling from Context Denoising Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.05862)
*Zecheng Tang,Baibei Ji,Juntao Li,Lijun Wu,Haijia Gui,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 长上下文模型（LCMs）在处理长序列方面展现出巨大潜力，但易受无关的“上下文噪声”干扰。本研究提出使用集成梯度（IG）分数来检测和量化噪声信息，并开发了一种名为上下文去噪训练（CDT）的策略。CDT能有效提升模型对关键信息的关注度及其对预测的影响。实验证明，CDT能显著提升模型性能，甚至使一个8B开源模型在某些任务上达到与GPT-4o相当的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文模型（LCMs）虽然在处理长序列方面表现出色，但容易受到上下文中无关信息的干扰，即“上下文噪声”，这会误导模型的注意力机制，影响其预测能力。因此，理解和解决上下文噪声问题对于提升LCMs的鲁棒性和实用性至关重要。

Method: 本研究首先对上下文噪声进行了细致的分析，并提出使用集成梯度（IG）分数作为一种有效的指标来检测和量化上下文中的噪声信息。基于对噪声的洞察，研究者提出了一种名为上下文去噪训练（CDT）的训练策略。CDT旨在通过识别并处理噪声，增强模型对关键信息的注意力，并强化这些关键信息对模型预测的影响。实验在四项任务上进行，涵盖了上下文窗口扩展和长上下文对齐两种设置，以验证CDT的有效性。

Result: 实验结果表明，即使是简单的上下文噪声缓解措施也能显著提升模型对关键信息的关注度，并带来积极的预测效益。所提出的CDT策略在多项任务和设置下均展现出优越性能。特别值得一提的是，一个采用CDT训练的8B开源模型在某项任务上的表现（50.92）已能与GPT-4o（51.00）相媲美，证明了CDT的有效性和潜力。

Conclusion: 本研究通过提出集成梯度（IG）分数来量化上下文噪声，并开发了上下文去噪训练（CDT）策略，有效解决了长上下文模型（LCMs）易受噪声干扰的问题。CDT不仅提升了模型对关键信息的关注度，还增强了这些信息对模型预测的贡献，并在多项基准测试中取得了显著成果，甚至能使中等规模模型达到先进水平。这表明CDT是一种有前景的LCMs训练方法，未来可进一步探索其在更广泛任务和模型上的应用，并研究更复杂的噪声模式及其缓解策略。

Abstract: Long-context models (LCMs) have demonstrated great potential in processing
long sequences, facilitating many real-world applications. The success of LCMs
can be attributed to their ability to locate implicit critical information
within the context for further prediction. However, recent research reveals
that LCMs are often susceptible to contextual noise, i.e., irrelevant tokens,
that can mislead model attention. In this paper, we conduct a fine-grained
analysis of the context noise and propose an effective metric, the Integrated
Gradient (IG) score, to detect and quantify the noise information within the
context. Our findings reveal that even simple mitigation of detected context
noise can substantially boost the model's attention on critical tokens and
benefit subsequent predictions. Building on this insight, we propose Context
Denoising Training (CDT), a straightforward yet effective training strategy
that improves attention on critical tokens while reinforcing their influence on
model predictions. Extensive experiments across four tasks, under both context
window scaling and long-context alignment settings, demonstrate the superiority
of CDT. Notably, when trained with CDT, an open-source 8B model can achieve
performance (50.92) comparable to GPT-4o (51.00).

### [41] [Hey, wait a minute: on at-issue sensitivity in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.12740)
*Sanghee J. Kim,Kanishka Misra*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“Divide, Generate, Recombine, and Compare”（DGRC）的新方法，利用“at-issueness”的概念来评估语言模型（LMs）在对话中的自然度。研究发现，LMs倾向于在“at-issue”内容上继续对话，并且这种倾向在经过指令微调的模型中更为明显。指令微调模型能够更好地识别并对“Hey, wait a minute”等提示词做出反应，从而调整其对话策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估语言模型（LMs）在对话中的自然度是一个挑战，因为“自然度”的定义多样且缺乏可扩展的量化指标。本研究旨在通过引入“at-issueness”这一语言学概念来解决这一问题，为衡量对话自然度提供一种新的、可量化的方法，并系统地测试语言模型在对话中的敏感行为。

Method: 研究提出了一种名为“Divide, Generate, Recombine, and Compare”（DGRC）的新方法。该方法首先将对话分割成子部分作为提示，然后利用LMs为这些子部分生成续写，接着将原始对话与生成的续写重新组合，最后比较重新组合序列的概率。此过程旨在减少语言分析中的偏差，并实现对对话敏感行为的系统测试。

Result: 研究发现，LMs在继续对话时更倾向于关注“at-issue”内容，并且这种倾向在经过指令微调的模型中表现得更为显著。此外，当对话中出现“Hey, wait a minute”等提示词时，LMs会降低对“at-issue”内容的偏好。虽然指令微调并未进一步增强这种对话提示的调节能力，但这种模式反映了成功的对话动态的典型特征。

Conclusion: DGRC方法为评估LMs的对话自然度提供了一种新颖且有效的方式，并通过“at-issueness”的概念揭示了LMs在对话中的倾向性行为。研究结果表明，LMs，特别是经过指令微调的模型，能够理解并适应对话中的细微线索，展现出更符合人类对话习惯的模式。这为开发更自然、更具交互性的对话AI提供了重要的见解。

Abstract: Evaluating the naturalness of dialogue in language models (LMs) is not
trivial: notions of 'naturalness' vary, and scalable quantitative metrics
remain limited. This study leverages the linguistic notion of 'at-issueness' to
assess dialogue naturalness and introduces a new method: Divide, Generate,
Recombine, and Compare (DGRC). DGRC (i) divides a dialogue as a prompt, (ii)
generates continuations for subparts using LMs, (iii) recombines the dialogue
and continuations, and (iv) compares the likelihoods of the recombined
sequences. This approach mitigates bias in linguistic analyses of LMs and
enables systematic testing of discourse-sensitive behavior. Applying DGRC, we
find that LMs prefer to continue dialogue on at-issue content, with this effect
enhanced in instruct-tuned models. They also reduce their at-issue preference
when relevant cues (e.g., "Hey, wait a minute") are present. Although
instruct-tuning does not further amplify this modulation, the pattern reflects
a hallmark of successful dialogue dynamics.

</details>


### [42] [DiscoTrack: A Multilingual LLM Benchmark for Discourse Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17013)
*Lanni Bu,Lauren Levin,Amir Zeldes*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 现有的LLM基准主要关注自然语言理解和显式信息提取（如问答、摘要），并且通常只针对单个句子。缺乏更具挑战性、尤其是多语言的基准，来关注跨越长文档的隐式信息和语用推理，以及话语跟踪（整合跨句子、段落和多说话者的话语信息）。为此，我们提出了DiscoTrack，一个涵盖12种语言和四个话语理解层面的LLM基准，包括显著性识别、实体跟踪、话语关系和桥接推理。我们的评估表明，即使是SOTA模型在这些任务上仍面临挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM基准主要侧重于自然语言理解中的显式信息提取，如问答和摘要，且通常局限于单个句子。这使得LLM在处理更复杂、跨越多句和段落的隐式信息、语用推理和多说话者对话方面能力不足。因此，需要一个更具挑战性、支持多语言且专注于话语跟踪的新型基准来评估LLM在这些方面的能力。

Method: 提出DiscoTrack基准，包含12种语言。该基准涵盖四个话语理解层面：1. 显著性识别（识别文本中最重要的信息）；2. 实体跟踪（跟踪对话中实体及其指代关系）；3. 话语关系（识别句子或段落之间的逻辑关系）；4. 桥接推理（理解隐含的关联）。通过设计相应任务来评估LLM在这些层面的表现。

Result: 评估结果显示，即使是当前最先进的模型在DiscoTrack基准的各项任务上仍然表现不佳，表明这些任务对LLM来说仍然具有挑战性。具体性能指标和模型间的比较有待在论文详细说明。

Conclusion: DiscoTrack基准的提出填补了现有LLM评估在处理跨文档隐式信息、语用推理和多语言话语跟踪方面的空白。现有SOTA模型在该基准上表现出的挑战性，凸显了在这些领域进一步提升LLM能力的重要性。未来的工作可以集中于改进模型以适应更复杂的话语理解任务，以及扩展基准的语言覆盖范围和任务复杂度。

Abstract: Recent LLM benchmarks have tested models on a range of phenomena, but are
still focused primarily on natural language understanding for extraction of
explicit information, such as QA or summarization, with responses often tar-
geting information from individual sentences. We are still lacking more
challenging, and im- portantly also multilingual, benchmarks focus- ing on
implicit information and pragmatic infer- ences across larger documents in the
context of discourse tracking: integrating and aggregating information across
sentences, paragraphs and multiple speaker utterances. To this end, we present
DiscoTrack, an LLM benchmark target- ing a range of tasks across 12 languages
and four levels of discourse understanding: salience recognition, entity
tracking, discourse relations and bridging inference. Our evaluation shows that
these tasks remain challenging, even for state-of-the-art models.

### [43] [A Survey on LLM Mid-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23081)
*Chengying Tu,Xuemiao Zhang,Rongxiang Weng,Rumei Li,Chen Zhang,Yang Bai,Hongfei Yan,Jingang Wang,Xunliang Cai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 近期，在基础模型训练中，一个名为“中期训练”的阶段被认为是连接预训练和后训练的关键环节。中期训练利用中间数据和计算资源，系统性地提升数学、编程、推理和长上下文扩展等特定能力，同时保持基础能力。本调查对大型语言模型（LLMs）的中期训练进行了形式化定义，并探讨了涵盖数据整理、训练策略和模型架构优化的框架。通过分析主流模型实现，说明中期训练在LLM能力渐进发展中扮演着独特且关键的角色，为LLM的未来研究和创新提供了全面的分类和可行性见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着基础模型在多阶段训练方面的进展，特别是“中期训练”的出现，它被发现是连接预训练和后训练的关键阶段。中期训练通过利用中间数据和计算资源，能够系统性地提升模型在数学、编程、推理和长上下文扩展等特定能力，同时又不损害模型的基础能力。因此，理解和优化这一阶段对于推进大型语言模型（LLMs）的发展至关重要。

Method: 本调查对大型语言模型（LLMs）的中期训练进行了形式化定义。研究了包含数据整理、训练策略和模型架构优化的优化框架。分析了主流模型在中期训练阶段的目标驱动干预措施，以说明中期训练在LLM能力渐进发展中的独特作用。

Result: 本调查分析了主流模型在中期训练阶段所采取的目标驱动干预措施。通过这些分析，论文阐释了中期训练如何作为LLM能力渐进发展中一个独特且关键的阶段。中期训练能够系统性地提升数学、编程、推理和长上下文扩展等特定能力，同时保持模型的基础能力。

Conclusion: 本调查通过明确中期训练的独特贡献，为大型语言模型（LLMs）的研究和创新提供了全面的分类和可行性见解。中期训练被证明是LLM能力发展中一个独特且关键的阶段，能够有效提升特定能力同时保持基础能力，为未来LLM的进一步发展指明了方向。

Abstract: Recent advances in foundation models have highlighted the significant
benefits of multi-stage training, with a particular emphasis on the emergence
of mid-training as a vital stage that bridges pre-training and post-training.
Mid-training is distinguished by its use of intermediate data and computational
resources, systematically enhancing specified capabilities such as mathematics,
coding, reasoning, and long-context extension, while maintaining foundational
competencies. This survey provides a formal definition of mid-training for
large language models (LLMs) and investigates optimization frameworks that
encompass data curation, training strategies, and model architecture
optimization. We analyze mainstream model implementations in the context of
objective-driven interventions, illustrating how mid-training serves as a
distinct and critical stage in the progressive development of LLM capabilities.
By clarifying the unique contributions of mid-training, this survey offers a
comprehensive taxonomy and actionable insights, supporting future research and
innovation in the advancement of LLMs.

### [44] [Leveraging Hierarchical Organization for Medical Multi-document Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23104)
*Yi-Li Hsu,Katelyn X. Mei,Lucy Lu Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了在医学多文档摘要（MDS）任务中引入层级结构化输入是否能优于传统的扁平化方法。研究发现，层级结构在保持事实性、覆盖面和连贯性的同时，提高了人类专家对模型生成摘要的偏好，并能提升摘要的清晰度。此外，研究还探讨了GPT-4模拟人类判断的有效性，发现其在更客观的评估维度上与人类判断有较高的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的医学多文档摘要（MDS）任务在处理跨文档关系时面临挑战，如何更有效地组织和情境化信息是关键问题。传统扁平化输入方法可能无法充分利用文档间的潜在层级关联，影响摘要质量。因此，研究旨在探索通过引入层级结构化输入来改善MDS模型的性能。

Method: 本研究探索了两种引入层级结构化信息的方法，并将其应用于三种大型语言模型（LLMs）。通过自动评估指标、基于模型的评估以及领域专家对摘要的偏好、可理解性、清晰度、复杂性、相关性、覆盖面、事实性和连贯性等方面的评估，对生成的摘要进行了全面的评估。此外，还研究了GPT-4模拟人类判断的一致性。

Result: 研究结果显示，人类专家更偏爱模型生成的摘要而非人工撰写的摘要。层级结构化方法在普遍保持事实性、覆盖面和信息连贯性的同时，显著增加了人类对摘要的偏好。GPT-4的模拟判断在更客观的评估维度（如事实性、覆盖面）上与人类判断表现出较高的一致性。

Conclusion: 研究证明，在医学摘要生成任务中引入层级结构能够提高模型生成摘要的清晰度，同时保持内容的覆盖面，是提升人类对生成摘要偏好的有效途径。这项工作为改进医学多文档摘要的质量和实用性提供了有价值的见解。

Abstract: Medical multi-document summarization (MDS) is a complex task that requires
effectively managing cross-document relationships. This paper investigates
whether incorporating hierarchical structures in the inputs of MDS can improve
a model's ability to organize and contextualize information across documents
compared to traditional flat summarization methods. We investigate two ways of
incorporating hierarchical organization across three large language models
(LLMs), and conduct comprehensive evaluations of the resulting summaries using
automated metrics, model-based metrics, and domain expert evaluation of
preference, understandability, clarity, complexity, relevance, coverage,
factuality, and coherence. Our results show that human experts prefer
model-generated summaries over human-written summaries. Hierarchical approaches
generally preserve factuality, coverage, and coherence of information, while
also increasing human preference for summaries. Additionally, we examine
whether simulated judgments from GPT-4 align with human judgments, finding
higher agreement along more objective evaluation facets. Our findings
demonstrate that hierarchical structures can improve the clarity of medical
summaries generated by models while maintaining content coverage, providing a
practical way to improve human preference for generated summaries.

### [45] [Zero-RAG: Towards Retrieval-Augmented Generation with Zero Redundant Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00505)
*Qi Luo,Xiaonan Li,Junqi Dai,Shuang Cheng,Xipeng Qiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLM）的幻觉问题通常通过检索增强生成（RAG）来缓解，但随着LLM内部知识的增长，外部语料库与LLM之间存在知识冗余，增加了检索成本并可能损害性能。本文提出了Zero-RAG框架，通过“Mastery-Score”指标识别并修剪冗余知识，并结合“Query Router”和“Noise-Tolerant Tuning”来减少不相关文档的干扰，从而更好地利用LLM的内部知识。实验表明，Zero-RAG可修剪30%的语料库，并将检索速度提高22%，同时不影响RAG性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）在生成内容时可能出现幻觉，检索增强生成（RAG）通过引入外部知识库来缓解此问题。然而，随着LLM内部知识的不断扩展，外部知识库与LLM的内部知识之间出现了显著的冗余。这种冗余不仅增加了密集检索的索引成本和计算负担，而且研究发现，过多的冗余信息甚至会干扰LLM对自身已知信息的调用，从而影响RAG的整体性能。因此，有必要解决这种知识冗余问题，以提高RAG的效率和效果。

Method: Zero-RAG框架包含三个主要部分：1. **Mastery-Score度量**: 该度量用于识别RAG语料库中的冗余知识。通过计算该分数，可以识别出LLM自身已经掌握（即“mastered”）的问题及其对应的知识，这些知识在外部语料库中是冗余的。2. **语料库修剪**: 基于Mastery-Score度量，对RAG的外部语料库进行修剪，移除冗余的知识条目。修剪后的语料库更精炼，只包含对LLM扩展知识或纠正幻觉至关重要的信息。3. **Query Router和Noise-Tolerant Tuning**: 为了在修剪后的语料库中更有效地利用LLM的内部知识并避免不相关文档的干扰，提出了Query Router来智能地路由查询，并采用了Noise-Tolerant Tuning来提高模型对噪声数据的鲁棒性，使其能够更好地利用内部知识。

Result: 实验结果表明，Zero-RAG框架在修剪Wikipedia语料库时，成功移除了30%的冗余内容。此外，该方法将检索阶段的速度提高了22%。重要的是，在实现这些效率提升的同时，并未对RAG的性能造成损害。这表明Zero-RAG在减少冗余、提高效率和保持性能之间取得了良好的平衡。

Conclusion: Zero-RAG通过引入Mastery-Score度量来识别和修剪RAG语料库中的冗余知识，并结合Query Router和Noise-Tolerant Tuning来增强LLM对内部知识的利用，有效解决了LLM知识扩展带来的RAG效率和性能问题。该方法在不牺牲性能的前提下，显著减少了语料库规模并加速了检索过程。未来的工作可以探索更精细的冗余识别方法，以及在更多样化的数据集和任务上验证Zero-RAG的有效性。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation has shown remarkable results to address Large
Language Models' hallucinations, which usually uses a large external corpus to
supplement knowledge to LLMs. However, with the development of LLMs, the
internal knowledge of LLMs has expanded significantly, thus causing significant
knowledge redundancy between the external corpus and LLMs. On the one hand, the
indexing cost of dense retrieval is highly related to the corpus size and thus
significant redundant knowledge intensifies the dense retrieval's workload. On
the other hand, the redundant knowledge in the external corpus is not helpful
to LLMs and our exploratory analysis shows that it instead hurts the RAG
performance on those questions which the LLM can answer by itself. To address
these issues, we propose Zero-RAG to tackle these challenges. Specifically, we
first propose the Mastery-Score metric to identify redundant knowledge in the
RAG corpus to prune it. After pruning, answers to "mastered" questions rely
primarily on internal knowledge of the LLM. To better harness the internal
capacity, we propose Query Router and Noise-Tolerant Tuning to avoid the
irrelevant documents' distraction and thus further improve the LLM's
utilization of internal knowledge with pruned corpus. Experimental results show
that Zero-RAG prunes the Wikipedia corpus by 30\% and accelerates the retrieval
stage by 22\%, without compromising RAG's performance.

</details>


### [46] [Multi-refined Feature Enhanced Sentiment Analysis Using Contextual Instruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00537)
*Peter Atandoh,Jie Zou,Weikang Guo,Jiwei Wei,Zheng Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为CISEA-MRFE的新型预训练语言模型（PLM）框架，用于改进在复杂情感场景下的情感分析性能。该框架通过上下文指令（CI）、语义增强增强（SEA）和多重精炼特征提取（MRFE）来解决现有方法在语义理解、泛化能力和数据不平衡方面存在的不足。实验结果表明，CISEA-MRFE在多个基准数据集上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于深度学习和预训练语言模型（PLM）的情感分析方法在处理细微情感线索、领域迁移和不平衡情感分布时表现不佳。研究认为这源于语义基础不足、对不同语言模式的泛化能力差以及对主要情感类别的偏见。因此，有必要提出一种能够克服这些挑战的新方法，以提高情感分析在复杂场景下的准确性和鲁棒性。

Method: 本研究提出了CISEA-MRFE框架，一个集成了上下文指令（CI）、语义增强增强（SEA）和多重精炼特征提取（MRFE）的新型PLM-based框架。CI通过注入领域感知指令来指导情感消歧；SEA利用情感一致的释义增强来提高模型的鲁棒性；MRFE结合了用于多尺度特征专业化的尺度自适应深度编码器（SADE）和用于情感感知序列建模的情感评估上下文编码器（EECE）。

Result: 在IMDb、Yelp、Twitter和Amazon四个基准数据集上的实验表明，CISEA-MRFE的准确率相较于强基线方法分别有高达4.6%、6.5%、30.3%和4.1%的相对提升。这些结果验证了该方法在跨领域情感分类的有效性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: CISEA-MRFE框架通过整合上下文指令、语义增强增强和多重精炼特征提取，有效解决了现有情感分析方法在处理复杂情感场景时遇到的挑战。实验结果证明了该方法的优越性和泛化能力，为未来在不同领域和复杂条件下的情感分析任务提供了有价值的解决方案。

Abstract: Sentiment analysis using deep learning and pre-trained language models (PLMs)
has gained significant traction due to their ability to capture rich contextual
representations. However, existing approaches often underperform in scenarios
involving nuanced emotional cues, domain shifts, and imbalanced sentiment
distributions. We argue that these limitations stem from inadequate semantic
grounding, poor generalization to diverse linguistic patterns, and biases
toward dominant sentiment classes. To overcome these challenges, we propose
CISEA-MRFE, a novel PLM-based framework integrating Contextual Instruction
(CI), Semantic Enhancement Augmentation (SEA), and Multi-Refined Feature
Extraction (MRFE). CI injects domain-aware directives to guide sentiment
disambiguation; SEA improves robustness through sentiment-consistent
paraphrastic augmentation; and MRFE combines a Scale-Adaptive Depthwise Encoder
(SADE) for multi-scale feature specialization with an Emotion Evaluator Context
Encoder (EECE) for affect-aware sequence modeling. Experimental results on four
benchmark datasets demonstrate that CISEA-MRFE consistently outperforms strong
baselines, achieving relative improvements in accuracy of up to 4.6% on IMDb,
6.5% on Yelp, 30.3% on Twitter, and 4.1% on Amazon. These results validate the
effectiveness and generalization ability of our approach for sentiment
classification across varied domains.

### [47] [SpecDiff-2: Scaling Diffusion Drafter Alignment For Faster Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00606)
*Jameson Sandler,Jacob K. Christopher,Thomas Hartvigsen,Ferdinando Fioretto*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SpecDiff-2提出了一种新颖的框架，通过使用离散扩散作为非自回归草稿生成器来解决潜在语言模型（LLM）推理中的两个关键瓶颈：自回归依赖性和草稿模型与验证模型之间的不匹配。该方法通过联合优化草稿和验证过程，在推理速度和准确性方面取得了显著的改进，在各种基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的投机解码方法在加速大型语言模型（LLM）推理方面存在两个主要瓶颈：1.草稿生成过程中的自回归依赖性限制了并行化，导致延迟。2.草稿模型和验证模型之间的不匹配导致频繁的草稿标记被拒绝，从而降低了效率。这些瓶颈阻碍了LLM推理的进一步加速，并限制了其在需要低延迟的应用中的实际部署。

Method: SpecDiff-2框架通过两个关键创新来解决上述瓶颈：（1）它采用离散扩散模型作为非自回归草稿生成器，以克服自回归依赖性限制并行化的第一瓶颈。离散扩散模型能够并行生成草稿标记，从而显著提高生成速度。（2）它开发了新颖的技术来校准离散扩散草稿模型与自回归验证模型。这有助于减少草稿和验证模型之间的不匹配，从而降低草稿标记被拒绝的频率，解决第二个瓶颈。实验在一个全面的基准套件上进行，以评估SpecDiff-2的性能。

Result: 在推理、编码和数学基准测试的综合基准套件上进行的实验表明，SpecDiff-2取得了最先进的成果。与现有基线相比，SpecDiff-2在每秒令牌数方面平均提高了55%，并且在标准解码方面平均实现了5.5倍的加速。重要的是，所有这些性能改进都是在不损失准确性的情况下实现的。

Conclusion: SpecDiff-2通过引入离散扩散作为非自回归草稿生成器，并开发了校准技术来解决草稿和验证模型之间的不匹配，成功地解决了投机解码中的两个关键瓶颈。该框架在推理速度和准确性方面均取得了显著的改进，并在各种基准测试中达到了新的最先进水平。这项工作为加速LLM推理提供了一种有效的方法，并为未来在投机解码领域的研究开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: Speculative decoding has become the standard approach for accelerating Large
Language Model (LLM) inference. It exploits a lossless draft-then-verify
procedure to circumvent the latency of autoregressive decoding, achieving
impressive speed-ups. Yet, current speculative decoding approaches remain
limited by two fundamental bottlenecks: (1) the autoregressive dependency
during drafting which limits parallelism, and (2) frequent rejections of draft
tokens caused by misalignment between the draft and verify models. This paper
proposes SpecDiff-2, a novel framework to jointly address these two
bottlenecks. It leverages discrete diffusion as a non-autoregressive drafter to
address bottleneck (1) and develops novel techniques to calibrate discrete
diffusion drafters with autoregressive verifiers, addressing bottleneck (2).
Experimental results across a comprehensive benchmark suite show that
SpecDiff-2 achieves a new state-of-the-art across reasoning, coding, and
mathematical benchmarks, improving tokens-per-second by up to an average of
+55% over previous baselines and obtaining up to 5.5x average speed-up over
standard decoding, without any loss of accuracy.

### [48] [Do Methods to Jailbreak and Defend LLMs Generalize Across Languages?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00689)
*Berk Atil,Rebecca J. Passonneau,Fred Morstatter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究首次系统性地评估了大型语言模型（LLMs）在十种不同语言（包括高、中、低资源语言）上的越狱攻击和防御的跨语言泛化能力。研究发现，攻击成功率和防御稳健性因语言而异，高资源语言在标准查询下更安全但在对抗性查询下更脆弱。简单的防御措施可能有效，但效果受语言和模型影响。研究强调了构建语言感知和跨语言安全基准的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLMs）在训练和微调后会进行安全对齐，但近期研究表明，越狱攻击可以绕过这些安全措施。然而，关于越狱攻击和防御措施的跨语言泛化能力的研究仍然不足，这是一个关键的研究空白，因为LLMs在全球范围内被广泛使用，其安全性不应局限于单一语言。

Method: 本研究对六种不同的LLMs在HarmBench和AdvBench基准上，跨越十种语言（涵盖高、中、低资源语言）进行了系统的多语言评估。研究评估了两种类型的越狱攻击：基于逻辑表达式的攻击和基于对抗性提示的攻击。

Result: 研究结果表明，越狱攻击的成功率和防御措施的稳健性在不同语言之间存在显著差异。具体来说，高资源语言在标准查询下表现出更高的安全性，但在面对对抗性查询时却更为脆弱。此外，研究发现，一些看似简单的防御措施在不同语言和模型上表现出不同的有效性，呈现出明显的语言和模型依赖性。

Conclusion: 本研究的发现强调了当前LLMs安全评估中跨语言能力不足的问题，并指出了现有防御措施的局限性。研究结果表明，需要开发更具语言感知能力和跨语言能力的LLM安全基准，以应对日益增长的全球化应用需求，并为构建更鲁棒、更安全的LLMs提供指导。未来的工作应集中于开发能够有效抵御跨语言越狱攻击的新型防御策略，并构建更全面的多语言安全评估框架。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) undergo safety alignment after training and
tuning, yet recent work shows that safety can be bypassed through jailbreak
attacks. While many jailbreaks and defenses exist, their cross-lingual
generalization remains underexplored. This paper presents the first systematic
multilingual evaluation of jailbreaks and defenses across ten languages --
spanning high-, medium-, and low-resource languages -- using six LLMs on
HarmBench and AdvBench. We assess two jailbreak types: logical-expression-based
and adversarial-prompt-based. For both types, attack success and defense
robustness vary across languages: high-resource languages are safer under
standard queries but more vulnerable to adversarial ones. Simple defenses can
be effective, but are language- and model-dependent. These findings call for
language-aware and cross-lingual safety benchmarks for LLMs.

### [49] [The Riddle of Reflection: Evaluating Reasoning and Self-Awareness in Multilingual LLMs using Indian Riddles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00960)
*Abhinav P M,Ojasva Saxena,Oswald C,Parameswari Krishnamurthy*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究首次系统性地评估了大型语言模型（LLMs）在七种主要印度语言（孟加拉语、古吉拉特语、印地语、卡纳达语、马拉雅拉姆语、泰米尔语和泰卢固语）上的文化推理和自我评估能力。研究发现，Gemini 2.5 Pro在解决谜语方面表现最佳，但模型在不同语言间的准确性存在显著差异。一个关键的发现是，模型的初始准确性与其识别自身错误的能力呈负相关：表现最好的模型（如Gemini 2.5 Pro）往往过于自信，而表现较差的模型（如LLaMA 4 Scout）则更具自我认知能力。研究强调了在多语言推理和模型自我反思能力方面存在的差距，并指出了开发既能有效推理又能认识自身局限性的模型的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLMs）在跨非英语语言的文化推理能力方面仍有待深入研究。本研究旨在填补这一空白，具体考察LLMs在七种主要印度语言上的推理和自我评估能力，以理解其在多语言和文化敏感场景下的表现，并揭示模型在自我认知方面的潜在问题。

Method: 研究团队首先构建了一个包含传统谜语及其变体的手写多语言谜语数据集，涵盖了七种印度主要语言。接着，他们选择了五种先进的LLMs（Gemini 2.5 Pro、Gemini 2.5 Flash、Mistral-Saba、LLaMA 4 Scout和LLaMA 4 Maverick）并在七种不同的提示策略下进行评估。评估分为两个阶段：第一阶段，模型被要求解决谜语，以衡量其推理能力；第二阶段，通过自我评估实验，测量模型在识别自身错误时的推理一致性。

Result: 在第一阶段的谜语解决任务中，Gemini 2.5 Pro总体表现最佳，但少样本学习（few-shot）策略仅带来边际效益，且模型在不同语言间的准确率差异显著。第二阶段的自我评估实验揭示了一个重要发现：模型的初始准确率与其识别自身错误的能力成反比。表现最强的模型（如Gemini 2.5 Pro）表现出过高的自信度（真实负例率仅为4.34%），而表现较弱的模型（如LLaMA 4 Scout）则展现出更高的自我反思能力（真实负例率高达42.09%）。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了当前LLMs在多语言文化推理方面存在的显著不足，并突显了模型在自我认知和纠错能力上的局限性。研究结果表明，简单提高模型性能并不足以保证其可靠性，因为高准确率模型可能缺乏自我反思能力。因此，未来的研究应致力于开发不仅能进行有效推理，还能准确评估自身局限性的LLMs，尤其是在处理多语言和跨文化内容时。

Abstract: The extent to which large language models (LLMs) can perform culturally
grounded reasoning across non-English languages remains underexplored. This
paper examines the reasoning and self-assessment abilities of LLMs across seven
major Indian languages-Bengali, Gujarati, Hindi, Kannada, Malayalam, Tamil, and
Telugu. We introduce a multilingual riddle dataset combining traditional
riddles with context-reconstructed variants and evaluate five LLMs-Gemini 2.5
Pro, Gemini 2.5 Flash, Mistral-Saba, LLaMA 4 Scout, and LLaMA 4 Maverick-under
seven prompting strategies. In the first stage, we assess riddle-solving
performance and find that while Gemini 2.5 Pro performs best overall, few-shot
methods yield only marginal gains, and accuracy varies notably across
languages. In the second stage, we conduct a self-evaluation experiment to
measure reasoning consistency. The results reveal a key finding: a model's
initial accuracy is inversely correlated with its ability to identify its own
mistakes. Top-performing models such as Gemini 2.5 Pro are overconfident (4.34%
True Negative Rate), whereas lower-performing models like LLaMA 4 Scout are
substantially more self-aware (42.09% True Negative Rate). These results point
to clear gaps in multilingual reasoning and highlight the need for models that
not only reason effectively but also recognize their own limitations.

</details>


### [50] [Tool-to-Agent Retrieval: Bridging Tools and Agents for Scalable LLM Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01854)
*Elias Lumer,Faheem Nizar,Anmol Gulati,Pradeep Honaganahalli Basavaraju,Vamse Kumar Subbiah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 现有的LLM多智能体系统在智能体选择时存在问题，因为检索方法通常匹配粗粒度的智能体描述，忽略了细粒度的工具功能。本文提出了一种名为“工具到智能体检索”的统一框架，它在共享向量空间中嵌入工具及其父智能体，并通过元数据关系将它们连接起来。这种方法能够进行细粒度的工具级或智能体级检索，避免了将多个工具聚合在一起造成的上下文稀释，并在LiveMCPBench基准测试中，在 आठ 种嵌入模型上均取得了显著的改进，Recall@5 提高了19.4%，nDCG@5 提高了17.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体系统在智能体选择时，依赖于粗粒度的智能体级描述进行检索，这忽略了底层工具的细粒度功能，导致智能体选择次优。当一个智能体管理大量工具或MCP服务器时，这种方法尤其会稀释上下文信息，影响检索效率和准确性。因此，需要一种能够同时兼顾工具和智能体信息，并进行细粒度检索的方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“工具到智能体检索”（Tool-to-Agent Retrieval）的统一框架。该框架的核心思想是在共享向量空间中同时嵌入工具及其父智能体，并利用元数据关系将它们联系起来。具体来说，它显式地表示工具的能力，并通过遍历元数据将信息传递到智能体层面。这使得检索系统能够进行细粒度的工具级或智能体级检索，确保智能体及其底层工具或MCP服务器得到同等程度的表示，而不会因为将许多工具打包在一起而导致上下文稀释。实验评估在LiveMCPBench基准测试上进行，并考察了八种不同的嵌入模型。

Result: 在LiveMCPBench基准测试上，与之前最先进的智能体检索器相比，本文提出的“工具到智能体检索”框架在 आठ 种嵌入模型上都取得了持续的性能提升。具体而言，Recall@5 指标提高了19.4%，nDCG@5 指标提高了17.7%。这些结果表明，该框架能够更准确地匹配查询到合适的工具和智能体。

Conclusion: “工具到智能体检索”框架通过在共享向量空间中联合表示工具和智能体，并利用元数据关系，成功解决了现有LLM多智能体系统中智能体选择的次优问题。该方法实现了细粒度的检索，提高了检索的准确性和效率，并且在实验中得到了验证。未来的工作可以进一步探索不同元数据关系的表示方式，以及在更广泛的多智能体场景中应用该框架。

Abstract: Recent advances in LLM Multi-Agent Systems enable scalable orchestration of
sub-agents, each coordinating hundreds or thousands of tools or Model Context
Protocol (MCP) servers. However, existing retrieval methods typically match
queries against coarse agent-level descriptions before routing, which obscures
fine-grained tool functionality and often results in suboptimal agent
selection. We introduce Tool-to-Agent Retrieval, a unified framework that
embeds both tools and their parent agents in a shared vector space and connects
them through metadata relationships. By explicitly representing tool
capabilities and traversing metadata to the agent level, Tool-to-Agent
Retrieval enables granular tool-level or agent-level retrieval, ensuring that
agents and their underlying tools or MCP servers are equally represented
without the context dilution that arises from chunking many tools together.
Evaluating Tool-to-Agent Retrieval across eight embedding models, our approach
achieves consistent improvements of 19.4% in Recall@5 and 17.7% in nDCG@5 over
previous state-of-the-art agent retrievers on the LiveMCPBench benchmark.

</details>

### [51] [Human-AI Co-Embodied Intelligence for Scientific Experimentation and Manufacturing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02071)
*Xinyi Lin,Yuyang Zhang,Yuanhang Gan,Juntao Chen,Hao Shen,Yichun He,Lijun Li,Ze Yuan,Shuang Wang,Chaohao Wang,Rui Zhang,Na Li,Jia Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“人-AI共体现智能”的新型物理AI范式，将人类用户、自主AI和可穿戴硬件融合，用于现实世界的实验和智能制造。该系统通过人类的精确执行和AI的记忆、推理、规划与反馈，弥合了机器智能与物理执行之间的差距，提高了实验的可重复性、可扩展性和可及性。研究中提出的APEX系统通过混合现实技术实现了对人类操作的观察、解释、标准操作流程对齐、3D视觉指导和实时错误纠正，并在柔性电子制造领域验证了其有效性，展现了超越通用多模态大语言模型的上下文感知推理能力，并能有效传授技能给新手。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学实验和制造依赖复杂的多步骤流程，需要人类持续的专业知识来进行精确执行和决策。尽管机器学习和自动化取得了进展，但传统模型仅限于虚拟领域，现实世界的实验和制造仍依赖人工监督。这种机器智能与物理执行之间的差距限制了科学和制造工作流程的可重复性、可扩展性和可及性。

Method: 研究提出了一种人-AI共体现智能的新范式，将人类用户、自主AI和可穿戴硬件集成在一起。在该体系结构中，人类负责精确执行和控制，而自主AI则提供记忆、上下文推理、自适应规划和实时反馈。可穿戴接口持续捕获实验和制造过程，促进人与AI之间的无缝通信，实现纠正性指导和可解释的协作。作为具体实现，研究提出了Agentic-Physical Experimentation (APEX)系统，通过混合现实技术将自主推理与物理执行相结合。APEX系统能够观察和解释人类行为，将其与标准操作规程对齐，提供3D视觉指导，并分析每一步操作。该系统在清洁室环境中用于柔性电子器件制造。

Result: 在柔性电子器件制造的实验中，APEX系统实现了上下文感知的推理，其准确性超过了通用多模态大语言模型。该系统能够实时纠正错误，并将专业知识传授给新手。研究结果表明，该系统能够将科学研究和制造转化为自主、可追溯、可解释和可扩展的过程。

Conclusion: 这项工作建立了一个新的自主-物理-人类智能类别，将自主推理扩展到计算领域之外，进入物理领域。该人-AI共体现智能范式有望彻底改变科学研究和制造，使其过程更加自主、可追溯、可解释和可扩展。未来的工作可以进一步探索该范式在更广泛的物理任务中的应用，并优化人与AI的交互方式。

Abstract: Scientific experiment and manufacture rely on complex, multi-step procedures
that demand continuous human expertise for precise execution and
decision-making. Despite advances in machine learning and automation,
conventional models remain confined to virtual domains, while real-world
experiment and manufacture still rely on human supervision and expertise. This
gap between machine intelligence and physical execution limits reproducibility,
scalability, and accessibility across scientific and manufacture workflows.
Here, we introduce human-AI co-embodied intelligence, a new form of physical AI
that unites human users, agentic AI, and wearable hardware into an integrated
system for real-world experiment and intelligent manufacture. In this paradigm,
humans provide precise execution and control, while agentic AI contributes
memory, contextual reasoning, adaptive planning, and real-time feedback. The
wearable interface continuously captures the experimental and manufacture
processes, facilitates seamless communication between humans and AI for
corrective guidance and interpretable collaboration. As a demonstration, we
present Agentic-Physical Experimentation (APEX) system, coupling agentic
reasoning with physical execution through mixed-reality. APEX observes and
interprets human actions, aligns them with standard operating procedures,
provides 3D visual guidance, and analyzes every step. Implemented in a
cleanroom for flexible electronics fabrication, APEX system achieves
context-aware reasoning with accuracy exceeding general multimodal large
language models, corrects errors in real time, and transfers expertise to
beginners. These results establish a new class of agentic-physical-human
intelligence that extends agentic reasoning beyond computation into the
physical domain, transforming scientific research and manufacturing into
autonomous, traceable, interpretable, and scalable processes.

### [52] [Deep Value Benchmark: Measuring Whether Models Generalize Deep values or Shallow Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02109)
*Joshua Ashkinaze,Hua Shen,Sai Avula,Eric Gilbert,Ceren Budak*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了深度价值基准（DVB），一个评估大型语言模型（LLMs）是否真正学习人类基本价值观而非仅仅表面偏好的框架。研究发现，现有模型在泛化深度价值观方面表现不佳，平均深度价值泛化率（DVGR）仅为0.30，且所有模型均低于随机水平，表明AI对齐方面存在严峻挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI对齐研究中的关键问题在于，大型语言模型（LLMs）是学习了人类的深层价值观，还是仅仅模仿了偏好数据中的表面模式。如果模型仅捕捉到表面模式，它们在面对新情境时可能无法稳健地泛化人类意图，从而导致行为失准。因此，区分和衡量模型对深层价值观的理解至关重要。

Method: 研究引入了深度价值基准（DVB），采用新颖的实验设计来分离深层价值（如道德原则）和浅层特征（如语言风格）。在训练阶段，模型接触到深度特征和浅层特征相关联的人类偏好数据（例如，用户倾向于选择“不作恶”且“语言正式”的选项而非“公正”且“语言非正式”的选项）。在测试阶段，这种关联被打破，模型需要选择（“公正”，正式语言）或（“不作恶”，非正式语言）的选项。这种设计使得研究人员能够精确测量模型的深度价值泛化率（DVGR），即模型基于潜在价值而非浅层特征进行泛化的概率。

Result: 在对9种不同模型进行的测试中，平均DVGR仅为0.30，所有模型的表现均低于随机猜测水平（0.5）。此外，研究还发现，规模更大的模型在DVGR方面表现略差于规模较小的模型。该研究发布了其数据集，该数据集经过了三项独立的人类验证实验。

Conclusion: DVB提供了一个可解释的指标，用于衡量AI对齐的核心特征——模型对人类深层价值观的理解和泛化能力。研究结果表明，当前的大型语言模型在理解和应用人类基本价值观方面存在显著不足，这对AI对齐研究提出了严峻挑战。未来的工作需要开发更有效的模型训练方法，以提升LLMs在价值观泛化方面的能力。

Abstract: We introduce the Deep Value Benchmark (DVB), an evaluation framework that
directly tests whether large language models (LLMs) learn fundamental human
values or merely surface-level preferences. This distinction is critical for AI
alignment: Systems that capture deeper values are likely to generalize human
intentions robustly, while those that capture only superficial patterns in
preference data risk producing misaligned behavior. The DVB uses a novel
experimental design with controlled confounding between deep values (e.g.,
moral principles) and shallow features (e.g., superficial attributes). In the
training phase, we expose LLMs to human preference data with deliberately
correlated deep and shallow features -- for instance, where a user consistently
prefers (non-maleficence, formal language) options over (justice, informal
language) alternatives. The testing phase then breaks these correlations,
presenting choices between (justice, formal language) and (non-maleficence,
informal language) options. This design allows us to precisely measure a
model's Deep Value Generalization Rate (DVGR) -- the probability of
generalizing based on the underlying value rather than the shallow feature.
Across 9 different models, the average DVGR is just 0.30. All models generalize
deep values less than chance. Larger models have a (slightly) lower DVGR than
smaller models. We are releasing our dataset, which was subject to three
separate human validation experiments. DVB provides an interpretable measure of
a core feature of alignment.

</details>


### [53] [Re-FORC: Adaptive Reward Prediction for Efficient Chain-of-Thought Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02130)
*Renos Zabounidis,Aditya Golatkar,Michael Kleinman,Alessandro Achille,Wei Xia,Stefano Soatto*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Re-FORC的自适应奖励预测方法，该方法能够根据上下文预测未来思考代币数量的预期未来奖励。Re-FORC通过训练一个轻量级适配器来改进推理模型，在更长的推理和更大的模型上表现出预测能力的提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理模型在处理需要长期规划和复杂推理的任务时，往往面临计算资源消耗大、推理效率低的问题。如何有效地预测和控制推理过程中的奖励，以优化计算资源的使用并提高推理的准确性，是一个重要的研究挑战。

Method: Re-FORC方法通过训练一个轻量级适配器来增强现有的推理模型。该适配器能够根据给定的上下文，预测未来思考代币数量与预期未来奖励之间的函数关系。通过这种方式，Re-FORC能够实现对推理过程的自适应控制。

Result: Re-FORC在多个方面展现了其优越性：1) 通过提前停止不具前景的推理链，在保持准确性的同时，计算量减少了26%。2) 通过优化模型选择和思考长度，在相同计算量下准确率提高了4%，在相同准确率下计算量减少了55%。3) 在测试时，自适应地调整计算量，在计算量大的情况下准确率提升11%，在计算量小的情况下准确率提升7%。

Conclusion: Re-FORC通过动态控制推理长度并预估计算时间，实现了对计算成本的有效管理和推理能力的提升。该方法为解决大规模模型和复杂推理任务中的计算效率和性能瓶颈提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: We propose Re-FORC, an adaptive reward prediction method that, given a
context, enables prediction of the expected future rewards as a function of the
number of future thinking tokens. Re-FORC trains a lightweight adapter on
reasoning models, demonstrating improved prediction with longer reasoning and
larger models. Re-FORC enables: 1) early stopping of unpromising reasoning
chains, reducing compute by 26% while maintaining accuracy, 2) optimized model
and thinking length selection that achieves 4% higher accuracy at equal compute
and 55% less compute at equal accuracy compared to the largest model, 3)
adaptive test-time scaling, which increases accuracy by 11% in high compute
regime, and 7% in low compute regime. Re-FORC allows dynamic reasoning with
length control via cost-per-token thresholds while estimating computation time
upfront.

</details>


### [54] [When One Modality Sabotages the Others: A Diagnostic Lens on Multimodal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02794)
*Chenyu Zhang,Minsol Kim,Shohreh Ghorbani,Jingyao Wu,Rosalind Picard,Patricia Maes,Paul Pu Liang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Despite advances in multimodal large language models (MLLMs), their reasoning processes are opaque, making it hard to determine modality influence, conflict resolution, and dominance. This paper introduces "modality sabotage," a failure mode where a high-confidence unimodal error misleads the model. To address this, a model-agnostic evaluation layer is proposed, treating each modality as an agent that produces candidate labels and self-assessments. A fusion mechanism then aggregates these outputs to identify contributing modalities and those that mislead. A case study on multimodal emotion recognition benchmarks with foundation models revealed systematic reliability profiles, offering insights into dataset artifacts versus model limitations. The framework provides a diagnostic scaffold for auditing multimodal reasoning and informing interventions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The opacity of reasoning traces in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) presents a significant challenge. It is often unclear which modality influences a prediction, how conflicting information from different modalities is resolved, or when one modality dominates the decision-making process. This lack of transparency hinders the understanding and improvement of MLLMs. The paper identifies a specific failure mode, "modality sabotage," where an error from a single modality, despite high confidence, overrides other evidence and leads to an incorrect fused output. Understanding and diagnosing such failures is crucial for developing more reliable and trustworthy MLLMs.

Method: The paper proposes a lightweight, model-agnostic evaluation layer to diagnose reasoning dynamics in MLLMs. This layer treats each modality as an independent agent. Each agent produces candidate labels for the task and a brief self-assessment of its confidence or reliability. A simple fusion mechanism then aggregates these individual modality outputs. This aggregation process allows for the identification of "contributors" (modalities supporting the correct outcome) and "saboteurs" (modalities that mislead the final prediction). The approach is applied as a diagnostic tool in a case study involving multimodal emotion recognition benchmarks using foundation models.

Result: In a case study on multimodal emotion recognition benchmarks, the application of the proposed diagnostic layer revealed systematic reliability profiles across different foundation models. These profiles provided valuable insights into the specific behaviors of each modality and how they contributed to or detracted from the overall prediction accuracy. The analysis helped to distinguish between failures arising from inherent dataset artifacts and those stemming from limitations within the models themselves. The results demonstrate the effectiveness of the diagnostic scaffold in auditing the fusion dynamics of MLLMs.

Conclusion: The proposed framework, centered around the concept of modality sabotage and employing a novel diagnostic evaluation layer, offers a principled approach to auditing the reasoning processes of multimodal large language models. By treating modalities as agents and analyzing their contributions and interferences, the diagnostic scaffold reveals systematic reliability profiles and sheds light on the causes of failures. This work not only provides a method for understanding complex fusion dynamics but also informs the development of targeted interventions to improve the robustness and trustworthiness of MLLMs. Future work could involve extending this framework to a wider range of multimodal tasks and exploring more sophisticated intervention strategies based on the diagnostic insights.

Abstract: Despite rapid growth in multimodal large language models (MLLMs), their
reasoning traces remain opaque: it is often unclear which modality drives a
prediction, how conflicts are resolved, or when one stream dominates. In this
paper, we introduce modality sabotage, a diagnostic failure mode in which a
high-confidence unimodal error overrides other evidence and misleads the fused
result. To analyze such dynamics, we propose a lightweight, model-agnostic
evaluation layer that treats each modality as an agent, producing candidate
labels and a brief self-assessment used for auditing. A simple fusion mechanism
aggregates these outputs, exposing contributors (modalities supporting correct
outcomes) and saboteurs (modalities that mislead). Applying our diagnostic
layer in a case study on multimodal emotion recognition benchmarks with
foundation models revealed systematic reliability profiles, providing insight
into whether failures may arise from dataset artifacts or model limitations.
More broadly, our framework offers a diagnostic scaffold for multimodal
reasoning, supporting principled auditing of fusion dynamics and informing
possible interventions.

</details>


### [55] [Personalized Decision Modeling: Utility Optimization or Textualized-Symbolic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02194)
*Yibo Zhao,Yang Zhao,Hongru Du,Hao Frank Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为ATHENA的自适应文本-符号以人为本的推理框架，用于解决个体决策模型与群体最优预测之间的差距。ATHENA通过两阶段方法，首先利用LLM发现群体层面的符号效用函数，然后进行个体层面的语义适应，创建个性化的语义模板来模拟个体选择。该框架在实际的出行模式和疫苗选择任务中表现出色，显著优于现有模型，F1分数提升至少6.5%。消融研究表明，两阶段方法均对提升预测性能至关重要。ATHENA将符号效用建模和语义适应有机结合，为模拟以人为本的决策提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的个体决策模型常常无法准确预测群体最优选择，特别是在疫苗接种等高风险情境下。这种偏差源于个体决策过程的独特性，它受到数值属性（如成本、时间）和语言影响（如个人偏好、约束）的共同作用。因此，需要一种能够有效整合这些信息并模拟个性化选择的模型。

Method: ATHENA框架包含两个主要阶段：1. 群体层面：利用LLM增强的符号发现技术，挖掘稳健的、群体层面的符号效用函数。2. 个体层面：在最优效用函数的指导下，进行个体层面的语义适应，生成个性化的语义模板，以模拟个体化的选择行为。该框架将效用理论与大型语言模型的文本推理能力相结合。

Result: 在实际的出行模式选择和疫苗接种选择任务中，ATHENA的预测性能得到了验证。相比于仅基于效用的模型、传统的机器学习模型以及其他基于LLM的模型，ATHENA的F1分数至少提高了6.5%，表现出显著的优越性。消融研究也证实，ATHENA的两个阶段（符号效用发现和语义适应）对于提升整体预测性能都至关重要且相辅相成，移除任何一个阶段都会导致性能明显下降。

Conclusion: ATHENA框架通过有机地整合符号效用建模和语义适应，为模拟以人为本的决策提供了一种创新的解决方案。该研究不仅在理论上填补了个体决策与群体最优预测之间的空白，而且在实践中通过在真实世界任务中的优异表现证明了其有效性。未来的工作可以进一步探索ATHENA在更广泛决策场景中的应用，并优化其在处理复杂语言影响和数值属性方面的能力。

Abstract: Decision-making models for individuals, particularly in high-stakes scenarios
like vaccine uptake, often diverge from population optimal predictions. This
gap arises from the uniqueness of the individual decision-making process,
shaped by numerical attributes (e.g., cost, time) and linguistic influences
(e.g., personal preferences and constraints). Developing upon Utility Theory
and leveraging the textual-reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models
(LLMs), this paper proposes an Adaptive Textual-symbolic Human-centric
Reasoning framework (ATHENA) to address the optimal information integration.
ATHENA uniquely integrates two stages: First, it discovers robust, group-level
symbolic utility functions via LLM-augmented symbolic discovery; Second, it
implements individual-level semantic adaptation, creating personalized semantic
templates guided by the optimal utility to model personalized choices.
Validated on real-world travel mode and vaccine choice tasks, ATHENA
consistently outperforms utility-based, machine learning, and other LLM-based
models, lifting F1 score by at least 6.5% over the strongest cutting-edge
models. Further, ablation studies confirm that both stages of ATHENA are
critical and complementary, as removing either clearly degrades overall
predictive performance. By organically integrating symbolic utility modeling
and semantic adaptation, ATHENA provides a new scheme for modeling
human-centric decisions. The project page can be found at

### [59] [When Modalities Conflict: How Unimodal Reasoning Uncertainty Governs Preference Dynamics in MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02243)
*Zhuoran Zhang,Tengyue Wang,Xilin Gong,Yang Shi,Haotian Wang,Di Wang,Lijie Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一个名为“模态跟随”的新框架，用于分析多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在面对冲突信息时如何做出决策。研究发现，模型跟随某一模态的概率与其相对推理不确定性呈负相关，并引入了“平衡点”的概念来衡量模型固有的模态偏好，解决了传统方法忽略模型置信度的问题。通过分析层级预测，揭示了模型在模糊区域的振荡机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究在衡量多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）处理冲突信息的能力时，仅依赖于粗粒度的数据集级别统计数据，未能深入探究模型在单模态推理中的置信度对其决策的影响。这导致了对模型行为的理解不够全面，无法准确评估和改进其在复杂多模态场景下的表现。因此，有必要提出一种更精细的分析框架，以揭示模型在模态冲突解决过程中的内在机制。

Method: 本研究引入了一个新的框架，将模态跟随分解为两个关键因素：相对推理不确定性（即模型在特定情况下对不同单模态预测的置信度差距）和固有的模态偏好（即在不确定性相似时模型表现出的稳定偏向）。为了验证该框架，研究构建了一个可控的数据集，系统地调整了视觉和文本输入的推理难度。研究使用熵作为精细化的不确定性度量指标，并通过分析层级预测来探究模型内部的振荡机制。

Result: 研究发现，模型跟随某一模态的概率随着该模态相对不确定性的增加而单调递减。在模型以相似概率跟随两种模态的“平衡点”处，可以观察到模型固有的模态偏好。这一测量方法比传统的宏观比例更具原则性且干扰更少，能够将模态偏好与其单模态能力和数据集偏差分离开来。此外，通过探测层级预测，研究揭示了在平衡点附近的模糊区域，模型会在不同层级之间摇摆，从而解释了外部观察到的犹豫不决现象。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了相对不确定性和固有偏好是支配模态跟随的两个核心原则，为多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）如何解决冲突信息提供了一个量化的框架和机制性的洞察。该研究不仅改进了对MLLMs行为的理解，还为未来开发更鲁棒、更可靠的多模态模型提供了方向。未来的工作可以进一步探索不同模态偏好对模型整体性能的影响，以及如何通过训练策略来调整和优化这种偏好。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) must resolve conflicts when
different modalities provide contradictory information, a process we term
modality following. Prior work measured this behavior only with coarse
dataset-level statistics, overlooking the influence of model's confidence in
unimodal reasoning. In this paper, we introduce a new framework that decomposes
modality following into two fundamental factors: relative reasoning uncertainty
(the case-specific confidence gap between unimodal predictions) and inherent
modality preference( a model's stable bias when uncertainties are balanced). To
validate this framework, we construct a controllable dataset that
systematically varies the reasoning difficulty of visual and textual inputs.
Using entropy as a fine-grained uncertainty metric, we uncover a universal law:
the probability of following a modality decreases monotonically as its relative
uncertainty increases. At the relative difficulty level where the model tends
to follow both modalities with comparable probability what we call the balance
point, a practical indicator of the model's inherent preference. Unlike
traditional macro-level ratios, this measure offers a more principled and less
confounded way to characterize modality bias, disentangling it from unimodal
capabilities and dataset artifacts. Further, by probing layer-wise predictions,
we reveal the internal mechanism of oscillation: in ambiguous regions near the
balance point, models vacillate between modalities across layers, explaining
externally observed indecision. Together, these findings establish relative
uncertainty and inherent preference as the two governing principles of modality
following, offering both a quantitative framework and mechanistic insight into
how MLLMs resolve conflicting information.

</details>


### [60] [Unlocking the Power of Multi-Agent LLM for Reasoning: From Lazy Agents to Deliberation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02303)
*Zhiwei Zhang,Xiaomin Li,Yudi Lin,Hui Liu,Ramraj Chandradevan,Linlin Wu,Minhua Lin,Fali Wang,Xianfeng Tang,Qi He,Suhang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）通过强化学习和可验证奖励在复杂推理任务上表现出色。本研究将此范式扩展到多智能体设置，其中一个元认知智能体提出计划并监控进度，而一个推理智能体通过顺序对话轮次执行子任务。尽管性能有所提高，但我们发现了一个关键限制：懒惰智能体行为，即一个智能体主导而另一个智能体贡献很少，破坏了协作并将设置简化为一个无效的单一智能体。为解决此问题，我们提出了一种衡量因果影响的稳定有效的方法，以缓解懒惰行为。此外，由于推理智能体容易在多轮交互中迷失方向并被之前的噪声响应所困，我们引入了一种可验证的奖励机制，允许推理智能体丢弃噪声输出、整合指令并在必要时重新启动其推理过程。实验证明，我们的框架减轻了懒惰智能体行为，并充分发挥了多智能体框架在复杂推理任务中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于多智能体协作的大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂推理任务中虽然取得了显著的成果，但存在一个关键的挑战，即“懒惰智能体行为”。在这种现象中，一个智能体倾向于承担大部分工作，而另一个智能体贡献甚少，这不仅破坏了智能体间的有效协作，还将原本的多智能体设置退化为低效的单智能体系统。这种行为的出现不仅影响了模型的整体性能，也限制了多智能体方法在解决复杂问题时的潜力，因此，研究并解决这一问题具有重要的理论和实践意义。

Method: 本研究首先对多智能体推理中懒惰行为的产生进行了理论分析。随后，提出了一种稳定且高效的因果影响度量方法来缓解这一问题。此外，为了解决推理智能体在多轮交互中可能迷失方向以及被噪声响应困扰的问题，研究引入了一种可验证的奖励机制。该机制旨在鼓励推理智能体进行反思，允许其丢弃不准确的输出、整合指令，并在必要时能够重新启动推理过程。

Result: 通过广泛的实验评估，证明了所提出的框架能够有效地缓解多智能体协作中的懒惰智能体行为。实验结果表明，该方法能够充分发挥多智能体框架在处理复杂推理任务时的潜力，显著提升了模型的整体性能和协作效率。

Conclusion: 本研究成功地识别并解决了多智能体大型语言模型（LLMs）中的懒惰智能体行为问题。通过引入新的理论分析、因果影响度量方法以及可验证的奖励机制，研究不仅缓解了协作中的不平衡现象，还增强了推理智能体的鲁棒性。实验结果有力地证明了所提出框架的有效性，为未来开发更强大、更可靠的多智能体推理系统奠定了基础。未来的工作可以进一步探索该机制在更广泛的多智能体任务中的应用，以及研究更精细化的智能体交互和激励策略。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) trained with reinforcement learning and
verifiable rewards have achieved strong results on complex reasoning tasks.
Recent work extends this paradigm to a multi-agent setting, where a
meta-thinking agent proposes plans and monitors progress while a reasoning
agent executes subtasks through sequential conversational turns. Despite
promising performance, we identify a critical limitation: lazy agent behavior,
in which one agent dominates while the other contributes little, undermining
collaboration and collapsing the setup to an ineffective single agent. In this
paper, we first provide a theoretical analysis showing why lazy behavior
naturally arises in multi-agent reasoning. We then introduce a stable and
efficient method for measuring causal influence, helping mitigate this issue.
Finally, as collaboration intensifies, the reasoning agent risks getting lost
in multi-turn interactions and trapped by previous noisy responses. To counter
this, we propose a verifiable reward mechanism that encourages deliberation by
allowing the reasoning agent to discard noisy outputs, consolidate
instructions, and restart its reasoning process when necessary. Extensive
experiments demonstrate that our framework alleviates lazy agent behavior and
unlocks the full potential of multi-agent framework for complex reasoning
tasks.

</details>

Abstract: Chronic Kidney Disease (CKD) affects nearly 10\% of the global population and
often progresses to end-stage renal failure. Accurate prognosis prediction is
vital for timely interventions and resource optimization. We present a

tokenization for continuous lab values and attention mechanisms for
interpretability. The model was pretrained with masked language modeling and
fine-tuned for binary classification tasks predicting progression from stage 3a
to stage 5 across varying follow-up and assessment periods. Evaluated on a
cohort of 91,816 patients, our model consistently outperformed CEHR-BERT,
achieving ROC-AUC up to 0.995 and PR-AUC up to 0.989 for short-term prediction.
These results highlight the effectiveness of transformer architectures and
temporal design choices in clinical prognosis modeling, offering a promising
direction for personalized CKD care.

### [62] [Generative World Models of Tasks: LLM-Driven Hierarchical Scaffolding for Embodied Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.04731)
*Brennen Hill*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Recent advances in agent development for complex multi-agent tasks like robotic soccer have focused on scaling models and data, but this end-to-end approach struggles with exploration and sparse rewards. This paper proposes that effective world models must capture both physics and task semantics. A review of 2024 research shows a trend towards integrating symbolic/hierarchical methods (HTNs, BSNs) with multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) to decompose goals and create intrinsic curricula. The authors formalize this into a framework for Hierarchical Task Environments (HTEs) that uses LLMs as generative world models for tasks. HTEs are argued to guide exploration, provide meaningful learning signals, and train agents with hierarchical structure, leading to more capable and sample-efficient agents compared to purely end-to-end methods.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: For complex, long-horizon multi-agent tasks such as robotic soccer, the predominant end-to-end approach of scaling model size and interaction data, while successful in other domains like large language models, often fails. This failure is attributed to intractable exploration spaces and the problem of sparse rewards, which hinder effective learning and agent development. The significance lies in the need for more sophisticated methods to enable agents to tackle intricate, strategic tasks that require long-term planning and coordination.

Method: The paper proposes a framework for Hierarchical Task Environments (HTEs) that integrates symbolic and hierarchical methods with multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). It draws upon a systematic review of 2024 research in low-resource multi-agent soccer, highlighting the trend of using techniques like Hierarchical Task Networks (HTNs) and Bayesian Strategy Networks (BSNs). The framework formalizes the integration of these methods, enabling the decomposition of complex goals into manageable subgoals, thereby creating an intrinsic curriculum for agent learning. Furthermore, Large Language Models (LLMs) are incorporated as generative world models capable of dynamically creating the necessary task scaffolding within the HTE framework.

Result: The paper argues that the proposed HTE framework, incorporating LLM-generated task structures, provides a mechanism to effectively guide exploration in complex task spaces. It facilitates the generation of meaningful learning signals and trains agents to internalize hierarchical structures. The authors contend that this approach leads to the development of more capable and general-purpose agents that exhibit greater sample efficiency compared to agents trained using purely end-to-end methods. While specific quantitative results are not detailed in the abstract, the claimed outcome is improved performance and learning efficiency.

Conclusion: The paper concludes that Hierarchical Task Environments (HTEs), augmented by LLMs for dynamic task scaffolding, are essential for bridging the gap between simple reactive behaviors and sophisticated strategic team play in multi-agent systems. This hierarchical approach offers a more effective way to train agents for complex, long-horizon tasks by addressing the limitations of sparse rewards and large exploration spaces inherent in purely end-to-end methods. The framework promises to enhance agent capability, generality, and sample efficiency, paving the way for more advanced multi-agent artificial intelligence.

Abstract: Recent advances in agent development have focused on scaling model size and
raw interaction data, mirroring successes in large language models. However,
for complex, long-horizon multi-agent tasks such as robotic soccer, this
end-to-end approach often fails due to intractable exploration spaces and
sparse rewards. We propose that an effective world model for decision-making
must model the world's physics and also its task semantics. A systematic review
of 2024 research in low-resource multi-agent soccer reveals a clear trend
towards integrating symbolic and hierarchical methods, such as Hierarchical
Task Networks (HTNs) and Bayesian Strategy Networks (BSNs), with multi-agent
reinforcement learning (MARL). These methods decompose complex goals into
manageable subgoals, creating an intrinsic curriculum that shapes agent
learning. We formalize this trend into a framework for Hierarchical Task
Environments (HTEs), which are essential for bridging the gap between simple,
reactive behaviors and sophisticated, strategic team play. Our framework
incorporates the use of Large Language Models (LLMs) as generative world models
of tasks, capable of dynamically generating this scaffolding. We argue that
HTEs provide a mechanism to guide exploration, generate meaningful learning
signals, and train agents to internalize hierarchical structure, enabling the
development of more capable and general-purpose agents with greater sample
efficiency than purely end-to-end approaches.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着生成模型在图像和文本领域的成功，对其进行评估变得越来越重要。现有的方法大多依赖于标量指标，而精确率-召回率（PR）曲线为评估提供了更丰富的视角，但其估计面临挑战。

Method: 提出了一种基于二元分类的PR曲线估计新框架，并进行了详细的统计分析，推导了PR估计风险的minimax上界。该框架能够扩展现有的PR指标，并应用于不同的实验场景。

Result: 该框架能够更全面地估计PR曲线，并提供了理论上的风险界限。实验结果表明，该框架在不同设置下均表现良好，并能揭示PR曲线的不同行为。

Conclusion: 本文提出的PR曲线估计新框架为生成模型的评估提供了一种更丰富、更鲁棒的方法。虽然该框架在理论和实验上都取得了积极成果，但未来仍可进一步探索其在更广泛模型和数据集上的应用，并优化计算效率。

Abstract: With the recent success of generative models in image and text, the question
of their evaluation has recently gained a lot of attention. While most methods
from the state of the art rely on scalar metrics, the introduction of Precision
and Recall (PR) for generative model has opened up a new avenue of research.
The associated PR curve allows for a richer analysis, but their estimation
poses several challenges. In this paper, we present a new framework for
estimating entire PR curves based on a binary classification standpoint. We
conduct a thorough statistical analysis of the proposed estimates. As a
byproduct, we obtain a minimax upper bound on the PR estimation risk. We also
show that our framework extends several landmark PR metrics of the literature
which by design are restrained to the extreme values of the curve. Finally, we
study the different behaviors of the curves obtained experimentally in various
settings.

### [65] [Auditable-choice reframing unlocks RL-based verification for open-ended tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02463)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将缺乏标准答案的开放式任务视为非推理场景，忽略了推理能力在这些任务中的潜力。本文旨在探索是否能通过加强推理来提升开放式任务的表现，并解决RLVR无法直接应用于开放域的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为VMR（Verifiable Multiple-Choice Reformulation）的新型训练策略。该策略将开放式数据重构为可验证的多项选择题格式，即使在没有明确 ground truth 的情况下也能进行有效训练。实验在多个基准测试中进行了验证。

Result: 在多个开放式任务基准测试中，VMR方法被证明能有效提升LLM的表现。与基线相比，VMR训练平均提高了5.99分。

Conclusion: VMR成功地将RLVR范式扩展到开放域，证明了加强推理能力对提升开放式任务表现的重要性。该方法在多个开放式任务上取得了显著的性能提升，为未来在开放域中利用RLVR开辟了道路。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has demonstrated great
potential in enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models
(LLMs), achieving remarkable progress in domains such as mathematics and
programming where standard answers are available. However, for open-ended tasks
lacking ground-truth solutions (e.g., creative writing and instruction
following), existing studies typically regard them as non-reasoning scenarios,
thereby overlooking the latent value of reasoning capabilities. This raises a
key question: Can strengthening reasoning improve performance in open-ended
tasks? To address this, we explore the transfer of the RLVR paradigm to the
open domain. Yet, since RLVR fundamentally relies on verifiers that presuppose
the existence of standard answers, it cannot be directly applied to open-ended
tasks. To overcome this challenge, we introduce Verifiable Multiple-Choice
Reformulation (VMR), a novel training strategy that restructures open-ended
data into verifiable multiple-choice formats, enabling effective training even
in the absence of explicit ground truth. Experimental results on multiple
benchmarks validate the effectiveness of our method in improving LLM
performance on open-ended tasks. Notably, across eight open-ended benchmarks,
our VMR-based training delivers an average gain of 5.99 points over the
baseline. Code will be released upon acceptance to facilitate reproducibility.

### [66] [Knowledge Graph-enhanced Large Language Model for Incremental Game PlayTesting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02534)

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 现代视频游戏更新频繁，给测试带来挑战。本文提出KLPEG框架，利用知识图谱（KG）系统建模游戏元素和依赖关系，并结合大语言模型（LLM）解析更新日志，通过多跳推理识别受影响的功能，生成针对性测试用例。实验证明KLPEG能更准确地定位更新影响范围，减少测试步骤，显著提升测试效率和效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代视频游戏迭代快、更新频繁，导致测试效率低下且不够精准。现有的基于大语言模型的自动化测试方法缺乏结构化的知识积累机制，难以针对增量更新进行精确高效的测试。这使得开发者难以快速验证更新内容，影响游戏质量和发布周期。

Method: KLPEG框架首先构建和维护一个知识图谱（KG），系统地对游戏元素、任务依赖关系和因果关系进行建模，从而实现跨版本知识的积累和复用。然后，该框架利用大语言模型（LLM）解析自然语言的游戏更新日志。通过在KG上进行多跳推理，识别出受更新影响的功能范围。最后，基于识别出的影响范围，生成针对特定更新的测试用例。

Result: 在Overcooked和Minecraft两个代表性游戏环境中进行的实验表明，KLPEG框架能够比现有方法更准确地定位受更新影响的功能。此外，KLPEG完成测试所需的步骤更少，显著提高了自动化游戏测试的有效性和效率。具体来说，KLPEG在定位影响范围和减少测试步骤方面表现出优势。

Conclusion: KLPEG框架通过结合知识图谱和大型语言模型，有效地解决了现代视频游戏频繁更新带来的自动化测试挑战。它通过结构化知识管理和智能分析，实现了更精准、高效的增量更新测试。未来工作可以探索将KLPEG应用于更复杂的游戏类型，以及进一步优化知识图谱的构建和推理能力，以应对更大规模和更动态的游戏更新。

Abstract: The rapid iteration and frequent updates of modern video games pose
significant challenges to the efficiency and specificity of testing. Although
automated playtesting methods based on Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown
promise, they often lack structured knowledge accumulation mechanisms, making
it difficult to conduct precise and efficient testing tailored for incremental
game updates. To address this challenge, this paper proposes a KLPEG framework.
The framework constructs and maintains a Knowledge Graph (KG) to systematically
model game elements, task dependencies, and causal relationships, enabling
knowledge accumulation and reuse across versions. Building on this foundation,
the framework utilizes LLMs to parse natural language update logs, identify the
scope of impact through multi-hop reasoning on the KG, enabling the generation
of update-tailored test cases. Experiments in two representative game
environments, Overcooked and Minecraft, demonstrate that KLPEG can more
accurately locate functionalities affected by updates and complete tests in
fewer steps, significantly improving both playtesting effectiveness and
efficiency.

### [67] [The ORCA Benchmark: Evaluating Real-World Calculation Accuracy in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02589)
*Claudia Herambourg,Dawid Siuda,Anna Szczepanek,Julia Kopczyńska,Joao R. L. Santos,Wojciech Sas,Joanna Śmietańska-Nowak*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了ORCA基准测试，一个评估大型语言模型（LLMs）在多领域、真实世界定量推理能力的新基准。该基准使用Omni计算引擎的验证输出来评估500个涵盖金融、物理、健康和统计等领域的自然语言任务。结果显示，包括ChatGPT-5、Gemini 2.5 Flash在内的五种最先进LLMs的准确率仅为45%-63%，主要错误集中在舍入（35%）和计算（33%）方面。ORCA基准测试能够评估LLMs的逐步推理、数值精度和跨领域泛化能力，并揭示了模型在特定领域的优势（数学、工程）和劣势（物理、自然科学），以及它们之间互补而非冗余的错误模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理涉及数字和计算的现实世界任务时，其定量推理能力仍然是一个严峻的挑战。现有的基准测试往往无法充分模拟真实世界问题的复杂性和多领域特性，也未能有效评估LLMs的逐步推理过程和数值精度。因此，有必要开发一个能够全面评估LLMs在多领域、真实世界定量推理能力的基准测试，以识别其当前的局限性并推动其改进。

Method: 本研究提出了ORCA（Omni Research on Calculation in AI）基准测试，该基准包含500个跨越金融、物理、健康和统计等多个领域的真实世界自然语言任务。这些任务的答案均由Omni计算引擎进行验证，以确保准确性。研究评估了五种先进的LLMs（ChatGPT-5、Gemini 2.5 Flash、Claude Sonnet 4.5、Grok 4和DeepSeek V3.2）在该基准上的表现。通过分析模型的准确率、错误类型（如舍入错误和计算错误）以及在不同领域的表现，并进行模型之间的相关性分析，来全面评估其定量推理能力，特别是逐步推理、数值精度和领域泛化能力。

Result: 在ORCA基准测试中，五种最先进的LLMs的准确率在45%到63%之间。错误分析显示，主要的错误来源是舍入错误（占35%）和计算错误（占33%）。在特定领域方面，模型在数学和工程领域表现较好，但在物理和自然科学领域存在明显劣势。模型间的相关性分析（r ≈ 0.40-0.65）表明，模型在错误类型上存在差异，呈现出一定的互补性，而非完全的冗余。这与标准数学数据集不同，ORCA更侧重于评估逐步推理、数值精度和跨领域泛化能力。

Conclusion: ORCA基准测试揭示了当前先进LLMs在多领域、真实世界定量推理方面存在的显著局限性，尤其是在处理舍入和计算错误方面。尽管模型在数学和工程领域表现出一定的优势，但在物理和自然科学等领域仍需改进。模型之间错误类型的差异表明它们具有一定的互补性，这为未来的模型融合和改进提供了方向。未来的研究应致力于提高LLMs在复杂定量推理任务中的准确性和鲁棒性，并进一步探索其在不同真实世界应用场景下的泛化能力。

Abstract: We present ORCA (Omni Research on Calculation in AI) Benchmark -- a novel
benchmark that evaluates large language models (LLMs) on multi-domain,
real-life quantitative reasoning using verified outputs from Omni's calculator
engine. In 500 natural-language tasks across domains such as finance, physics,
health, and statistics, the five state-of-the-art systems (ChatGPT-5,
Gemini~2.5~Flash, Claude~Sonnet~4.5, Grok~4, and DeepSeek~V3.2) achieved only
$45\text{--}63\,\%$ accuracy, with errors mainly related to rounding ($35\,\%$)
and calculation mistakes ($33\,\%$). Results in specific domains indicate
strengths in mathematics and engineering, but weaknesses in physics and natural
sciences. Correlation analysis ($r \approx 0.40\text{--}0.65$) shows that the
models often fail together but differ in the types of errors they make,
highlighting their partial complementarity rather than redundancy. Unlike
standard math datasets, ORCA evaluates step-by-step reasoning, numerical
precision, and domain generalization across real problems from finance,
physics, health, and statistics.

</details>

### [69] [DecompSR: A dataset for decomposed analyses of compositional multihop spatial reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02627)
*Lachlan McPheat,Navdeep Kaur,Robert Blackwell,Alessandra Russo,Anthony G. Cohn,Pranava Madhyastha*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DecompSR是一个包含超过500万个数据点的大型基准数据集和生成框架，用于分析大型语言模型（LLMs）在组合空间推理方面的能力。该数据集允许独立调整推理深度、实体和语言可变性、输入顺序和干扰项，以及新语言元素的组合度。实验表明，LLMs在生产性和系统性泛化方面存在困难，但在语言变化方面表现更好。DecompSR提供了一个可证明正确且严格的基准测试数据集，能够精细地探测LLMs的组合推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基准测试未能充分评估大型语言模型（LLMs）在组合空间推理方面的能力。本研究旨在创建一个能够精细探测LLMs组合推理能力的数据集，以揭示其在处理复杂空间关系时的局限性。

Method: 本研究引入DecompSR，一个包含超过500万个数据点的大型基准数据集和生成框架。DecompSR通过程序化方式生成，确保其“正确性即构造”，并通过符号求解器进行独立验证，以保证数据集的正确性。该框架允许独立调整组合性的各个方面：生产性（推理深度）、可替代性（实体和语言可变性）、过度泛化（输入顺序、干扰项）和系统性（新语言元素）。研究人员使用DecompSR对多个LLMs进行了基准测试。

Result: 通过在DecompSR数据集上对LLMs进行基准测试，研究发现LLMs在处理生产性和系统性泛化方面存在显著困难，尤其是在空间推理任务中。然而，LLMs在应对语言可变性方面表现出更强的鲁棒性。这意味着模型在理解和生成复杂推理链条方面存在不足，但在适应不同的语言表达方式时能力更强。

Conclusion: DecompSR提供了一个可证明正确且严格的基准测试数据集，并且能够独立调整组合性的关键方面，从而能够对LLMs的组合推理能力进行稳健且细粒度的探测。研究结果表明，尽管LLMs在语言适应性方面表现良好，但在生产性和系统性空间推理方面仍有待改进。未来的工作可以利用DecompSR来开发更强大的LLMs，以提高其组合推理能力。

Abstract: We introduce DecompSR, decomposed spatial reasoning, a large benchmark
dataset (over 5m datapoints) and generation framework designed to analyse
compositional spatial reasoning ability. The generation of DecompSR allows
users to independently vary several aspects of compositionality, namely:
productivity (reasoning depth), substitutivity (entity and linguistic
variability), overgeneralisation (input order, distractors) and systematicity
(novel linguistic elements). DecompSR is built procedurally in a manner which
makes it is correct by construction, which is independently verified using a
symbolic solver to guarantee the correctness of the dataset. DecompSR is
comprehensively benchmarked across a host of Large Language Models (LLMs) where
we show that LLMs struggle with productive and systematic generalisation in
spatial reasoning tasks whereas they are more robust to linguistic variation.
DecompSR provides a provably correct and rigorous benchmarking dataset with a
novel ability to independently vary the degrees of several key aspects of
compositionality, allowing for robust and fine-grained probing of the
compositional reasoning abilities of LLMs.

</details>


### [70] [CostBench: Evaluating Multi-Turn Cost-Optimal Planning and Adaptation in Dynamic Environments for LLM Tool-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02734)
*Jiayu Liu,Cheng Qian,Zhaochen Su,Qing Zong,Shijue Huang,Bingxiang He,Yi R. Fung*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 当前对大型语言模型（LLM）智能体的评估主要关注任务完成情况，忽视了资源效率和适应性。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了CostBench，一个以成本为中心的基准测试，用于评估智能体的经济推理和重新规划能力。CostBench包含在旅行规划领域，提供多种工具和可定制的成本，并模拟动态变化（如工具故障和成本变更），以评估智能体的实时适应能力。评估结果显示，当前智能体在成本优化规划方面存在显著差距，即使是GPT-5在最难任务上的精确匹配率也低于75%，在动态条件下性能下降约40%。CostBench为开发经济理性且鲁棒的智能体奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLM）智能体评估方法主要侧重于任务完成能力，而忽视了智能体在资源效率和适应性方面的表现。然而，在现实世界中，智能体需要能够制定并根据不断变化的环境调整成本最优的计划。这种成本意识和动态适应能力对于LLM智能体的实际应用至关重要，但目前缺乏专门的评估基准来衡量这些方面。因此，有必要开发一个能够系统性评估LLM智能体经济推理和重新规划能力的基准，以弥补当前评估方法的不足。

Method: 为了评估LLM智能体在成本优化规划和动态适应方面的能力，我们提出了CostBench基准测试。CostBench在旅行规划领域设计了多种任务，这些任务可以通过不同的原子和复合工具序列来解决，并且这些工具具有多样化且可定制的成本。为了模拟真实世界的不可预测性，CostBench包含了四种类型的动态阻塞事件，例如工具故障和成本变化，这迫使智能体在实时环境中进行适应和重新规划。我们使用包括开源和专有模型在内的领先LLM智能体在CostBench上进行了评估，以测试它们在静态和动态环境下的表现。

Result: 在CostBench基准测试上的评估结果表明，当前的LLM智能体在成本优化规划方面存在显著的不足。在静态环境下，智能体频繁未能识别出成本最优的解决方案。具体而言，即使是最先进的模型，如GPT-5，在处理最困难的任务时，其精确匹配率也低于75%。更令人担忧的是，当引入动态条件（如工具故障或成本变化）时，智能体的性能会进一步下降约40%。这表明LLM智能体在面对实际应用中常见的不可预测性和资源限制时，其鲁棒性和经济理性表现不足。

Conclusion: CostBench的提出填补了LLM智能体评估领域的一个重要空白，即缺乏对经济推理和动态适应能力的系统性衡量。通过在旅行规划领域引入具有成本敏感性和动态性的任务，CostBench揭示了当前LLM智能体在成本优化规划方面的显著差距，尤其是在动态和不可预测的环境下。研究结果表明，未来的LLM智能体需要重点提升其经济理性决策和实时重规划能力。CostBench为未来开发更高效、更鲁棒的LLM智能体提供了重要的评估平台和研究方向，尽管其局限于旅行规划领域，但其方法论可推广至其他需要成本优化和动态适应的场景。

Abstract: Current evaluations of Large Language Model (LLM) agents primarily emphasize
task completion, often overlooking resource efficiency and adaptability. This
neglects a crucial capability: agents' ability to devise and adjust
cost-optimal plans in response to changing environments. To bridge this gap, we
introduce CostBench, a scalable, cost-centric benchmark designed to evaluate
agents' economic reasoning and replanning abilities. Situated in the
travel-planning domain, CostBench comprises tasks solvable via multiple
sequences of atomic and composite tools with diverse, customizable costs. It
also supports four types of dynamic blocking events, such as tool failures and
cost changes, to simulate real-world unpredictability and necessitate agents to
adapt in real time. Evaluating leading open-sourced and proprietary models on
CostBench reveals a substantial gap in cost-aware planning: agents frequently
fail to identify cost-optimal solutions in static settings, with even GPT-5
achieving less than 75% exact match rate on the hardest tasks, and performance
further dropping by around 40% under dynamic conditions. By diagnosing these
weaknesses, CostBench lays the groundwork for developing future agents that are
both economically rational and robust.
